### Development Step 4: Locate 1851 Atheistic Naturalism Phrenology Mesmerism Book and 2009 Reissuing Publisher

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify a co-authored book from 1851 that advocated for atheistic naturalism, systematically explored phrenology and mesmerism, was controversial for these topics, and was reissued by a publisher in 2009. Search using keywords including '1851 book atheistic naturalism phrenology mesmerism co-authored', '1851 controversial book phrenology mesmerism reissued 2009', 'atheistic naturalism 1851 publication', and 'phrenology mesmerism 1851 authors'. Focus on identifying both the original 1851 publication details and the specific publisher who reissued it in 2009.

**Use Cases**:
- University research library digitization team using the multi-engine search script to locate and verify obscure 1851 scientific texts for digital archive inclusion and confirm 2009 reissue details.
- Historical society librarian employing automated Google Scholar, Bing, JSTOR, and archive.org queries to compile a complete bibliography of co-authored controversial phrenology and mesmerism treatises for a museum exhibition.
- Digital humanities scholar mapping the spread of atheistic naturalism by systematically harvesting primary sources and modern reprint information from multiple search engines for network analysis.
- Rare bookseller validating a potential 1851 first edition‚Äôs provenance by cross-referencing academic databases and general web searches to confirm authorship, publication history, and a 2009 specialty press reissue.
- PhD candidate in history of science leveraging the Python multi-method search to uncover mid-19th century philosophical works on phrenology and mesmerism across library catalogs and online archives for dissertation research.
- Independent publisher‚Äôs research team discovering forgotten public domain texts for annotated reissues by scanning academic sites and search engines to identify obscure co-authored volumes and track modern rights holders.
- Data journalist investigating the revival of fringe-science publications by extracting publication metadata and reissue patterns from search logs to illustrate how 19th-century controversial works reappear in contemporary niche markets.

```
import os
import requests
import json
import time
from urllib.parse import quote_plus
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

print('=== ALTERNATIVE SEARCH STRATEGY FOR 1851 ATHEISTIC NATURALISM BOOK ===')
print('Previous attempts failed due to API rate limits (SERPAPI) and HTTP 202 responses (DuckDuckGo)')
print('Implementing multi-pronged approach with different search engines and methods\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# Initialize comprehensive results storage
search_results = {
'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'objective': 'Find 1851 co-authored book on atheistic naturalism with phrenology/mesmerism, reissued 2009',
'search_methods': [],
'all_findings': [],
'book_candidates': [],
'analysis_summary': {}
}

print('TARGET BOOK CHARACTERISTICS:')
print('‚Ä¢ Published: 1851')
print('‚Ä¢ Co-authored (multiple authors)')
print('‚Ä¢ Topic: Atheistic naturalism')
print('‚Ä¢ Contains: Phrenology and mesmerism content')
print('‚Ä¢ Controversial for these topics')
print('‚Ä¢ Reissued by a publisher in 2009')
print()

# Method 1: Try Google Scholar search using requests
print('=== METHOD 1: GOOGLE SCHOLAR DIRECT SEARCH ===')
print('=' * 60)

scholar_queries = [
'"atheistic naturalism" 1851 phrenology mesmerism',
'1851 controversial book phrenology mesmerism authors',
'phrenology mesmerism 1851 naturalism philosophy'
]

headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36',
'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8',
'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9',
'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate, br',
'Connection': 'keep-alive'
}

for i, query in enumerate(scholar_queries, 1):
print(f'\nGoogle Scholar Search {i}: {query}')
try:
scholar_url = f'https://scholar.google.com/scholar?q={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {scholar_url}')

response = requests.get(scholar_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
# Save raw HTML
filename = f'google_scholar_search_{i}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)
with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)
print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Quick parse for academic results
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Look for result titles in Google Scholar
result_titles = soup.find_all(['h3', 'a'], class_=lambda x: x and 'gs_rt' in str(x))
if not result_titles:
result_titles = soup.find_all('h3')

print(f'Found {len(result_titles)} potential results')

for j, title_elem in enumerate(result_titles[:5], 1):
title_text = title_elem.get_text().strip()
if len(title_text) > 10:
print(f' {j}. {title_text[:100]}...')

# Check for key terms
text_lower = title_text.lower()
relevance_indicators = []
if '1851' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('1851')
if 'phrenology' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('phrenology')
if 'mesmerism' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('mesmerism')
if 'naturalism' in text_lower: relevance_indicators.append('naturalism')

if relevance_indicators:
print(f' ‚≠ê Relevant terms: {', '.join(relevance_indicators)}')
search_results['all_findings'].append({
'source': 'Google Scholar',
'query': query,
'title': title_text,
'relevance_terms': relevance_indicators,
'method': 'scholar_direct'
})

search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google Scholar: {query} - Status {response.status_code}')
else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting

# Method 2: Try Bing search
print('\n=== METHOD 2: BING SEARCH ===')
print('=' * 40)

bing_queries = [
'"1851" "atheistic naturalism" phrenology mesmerism book',
'1851 controversial phrenology mesmerism co-authored book',
'phrenology mesmerism 1851 naturalism reissued 2009'
]

for i, query in enumerate(bing_queries, 1):
print(f'\nBing Search {i}: {query}')
try:
bing_url = f'https://www.bing.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {bing_url}')

response = requests.get(bing_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
# Save raw HTML
filename = f'bing_search_{i}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)
with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)
print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Parse for results
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Look for Bing result titles
result_links = soup.find_all('a', href=True)
relevant_results = []

for link in result_links:
link_text = link.get_text().strip()
href = link.get('href')

if len(link_text) > 15 and href:
text_lower = link_text.lower()
relevance_score = 0
matched_terms = []

key_terms = {'1851': 3, 'phrenology': 2, 'mesmerism': 2, 'naturalism': 2, 'atheistic': 2, 'book': 1}

for term, weight in key_terms.items():
if term in text_lower:
relevance_score += weight
matched_terms.append(term)

if relevance_score >= 3:
relevant_results.append({
'text': link_text[:150],
'href': href,
'score': relevance_score,
'terms': matched_terms
})

print(f'Found {len(relevant_results)} relevant results')
for j, result in enumerate(relevant_results[:3], 1):
print(f' {j}. Score {result["score"]}: {result["text"]}...')
print(f' Terms: {', '.join(result["terms"])}')

search_results['all_findings'].append({
'source': 'Bing',
'query': query,
'title': result['text'],
'link': result['href'],
'relevance_score': result['score'],
'relevance_terms': result['terms'],
'method': 'bing_direct'
})

search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Bing: {query} - Status {response.status_code}')
else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting

# Method 3: Try specific academic database searches
print('\n=== METHOD 3: ACADEMIC DATABASE SEARCHES ===')
print('=' * 50)

# Try JSTOR, Project MUSE, and other academic sources
academic_sites = [
'site:jstor.org',

'site:archive.org',
'site:hathitrust.org'
]

base_query = '1851 atheistic naturalism phrenology mesmerism'

for i, site in enumerate(academic_sites, 1):
query = f'{site} {base_query}'
print(f'\nAcademic Search {i}: {query}')

try:
# Use Google to search specific academic sites
google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {google_url}')

response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
filename = f'academic_search_{i}_{site.replace("site:", "").replace(".", "_")}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)
with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)
print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Quick analysis
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Look for Google result snippets
snippets = soup.find_all(['span', 'div'], class_=lambda x: x and 'st' in str(x).lower())

relevant_snippets = []
for snippet in snippets:
snippet_text = snippet.get_text().strip()
if len(snippet_text) > 20:
text_lower = snippet_text.lower()
if any(term in text_lower for term in ['1851', 'phrenology', 'mesmerism', 'naturalism']):
relevant_snippets.append(snippet_text[:200])

print(f'Found {len(relevant_snippets)} relevant snippets')
for j, snippet in enumerate(relevant_snippets[:2], 1):
print(f' {j}. {snippet}...')

search_results['all_findings'].append({
'source': f'Academic - {site}',
'query': query,
'snippet': snippet,
'method': 'academic_site_search'
})

search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Academic {site}: Status {response.status_code}')
else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(4) # Longer delay for Google

# Method 4: Try alternative search engines
print('\n=== METHOD 4: ALTERNATIVE SEARCH ENGINES ===')
print('=' * 50)

# Try Startpage (uses Google results but with privacy)

print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
filename = 'startpage_search.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)
with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)
print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Startpage: Status {response.status_code}')
else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

# Analyze all findings
print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF ALL SEARCH METHODS')
print('=' * 80)

total_findings = len(search_results['all_findings'])
print(f'Total findings collected: {total_findings}')
print(f'Search methods attempted: {len(search_results["search_methods"])}')

if search_results['all_findings']:
print('\nüîç ALL FINDINGS ANALYSIS:')
print('-' * 40)

# Group by source
by_source = {}
for finding in search_results['all_findings']:
source = finding['source']
if source not in by_source:
by_source[source] = []
by_source[source].append(finding)

for source, findings in by_source.items():
print(f'\n{source} ({len(findings)} findings):')
for i, finding in enumerate(findings, 1):
title = finding.get('title', finding.get('snippet', 'No title'))[:100]
terms = finding.get('relevance_terms', [])
score = finding.get('relevance_score', 'N/A')
print(f' {i}. {title}... (Score: {score}, Terms: {", ".join(terms)})')

# Identify potential book candidates
book_indicators = ['book', 'work', 'treatise', 'publication', 'volume']
year_indicators = ['1851']
topic_indicators = ['phrenology', 'mesmerism', 'naturalism', 'atheistic']

for finding in search_results['all_findings']:
text_content = (finding.get('title', '') + ' ' + finding.get('snippet', '')).lower()

has_book = any(indicator in text_content for indicator in book_indicators)
has_year = any(indicator in text_content for indicator in year_indicators)
has_topic = any(indicator in text_content for indicator in topic_indicators)

if has_book and has_year and has_topic:
search_results['book_candidates'].append(finding)

print(f'\nüìö POTENTIAL BOOK CANDIDATES: {len(search_results["book_candidates"])}')
for i, candidate in enumerate(search_results['book_candidates'], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. Source: {candidate["source"]}')
print(f' Title/Snippet: {candidate.get("title", candidate.get("snippet", "No content"))[:150]}...')
print(f' Terms: {candidate.get("relevance_terms", [])}')
print(f' Score: {candidate.get("relevance_score", "N/A")}')

else:
print('\n‚ùå No findings collected from any search method')
print('This suggests the book may be:')
print('1. Very obscure or not well-digitized')
print('2. Known by a different title or description')
print('3. Not matching our exact search terms')

# Save comprehensive results
results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'comprehensive_1851_book_search.json')
with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}')

# Summary statistics
search_results['analysis_summary'] = {
'total_findings': total_findings,
'book_candidates': len(search_results['book_candidates']),
'search_methods_attempted': len(search_results['search_methods']),
'successful_searches': len([m for m in search_results['search_methods'] if '200' in m]),
'sources_used': list(set([f['source'] for f in search_results['all_findings']])) if search_results['all_findings'] else []
}

print(f'\nüìä FINAL SEARCH STATISTICS:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total findings: {search_results["analysis_summary"]["total_findings"]}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Book candidates: {search_results["analysis_summary"]["book_candidates"]}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Methods attempted: {search_results["analysis_summary"]["search_methods_attempted"]}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {search_results["analysis_summary"]["successful_searches"]}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Sources accessed: {search_results["analysis_summary"]["sources_used"]}')

print('\nüéØ RECOMMENDED NEXT STEPS:')
if search_results['book_candidates']:
print('1. ‚úÖ Investigate specific book candidates found')
print('2. ‚úÖ Follow up on promising links and sources')
print('3. ‚úÖ Search for 2009 reissue information')
else:
print('1. üîÑ Try more specific author name searches')
print('2. üîÑ Search for "controversial 1851 books" generally')
print('3. üîÑ Look into 19th century philosophy/science book catalogs')
print('4. üîÑ Search academic databases for phrenology/mesmerism history')

print('5. üìã Review all saved HTML files for additional context')
print('6. üîç Consider library catalog searches (WorldCat, etc.)')

print('\n=== COMPREHENSIVE MULTI-METHOD SEARCH COMPLETE ===')

### Development Step 8: Locate 1851 atheistic naturalism book on phrenology & mesmerism reissued by publisher in 2009

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify a co-authored book from 1851 that advocated for atheistic naturalism, systematically explored phrenology and mesmerism, was controversial for these topics, and was reissued by a publisher in 2009. Search using keywords including '1851 book atheistic naturalism phrenology mesmerism co-authored', '1851 controversial book phrenology mesmerism reissued 2009', 'atheistic naturalism 1851 publication', and 'phrenology mesmerism 1851 authors'. Focus on identifying both the original 1851 publication details and the specific publisher who reissued it in 2009.

**Use Cases**:
- Academic historian cataloging 19th-century controversial publications by extracting author names, thematic keywords (e.g., ‚Äúatheistic naturalism,‚Äù ‚Äúphrenology‚Äù), and original/reissue dates from archived HTML search results to build a digital bibliography.
- Legal e-discovery team automating the analysis of thousands of saved HTML case summaries to identify specific statutes, publication years, and co-counsel mentions for evidence tracking in litigation.
- Publishing house digital archivist processing legacy website snapshots to pinpoint out-of-print titles, detect reissue editions (e.g., 2009 reprints), and extract publisher credits for planning new annotated volumes.
- Marketing intelligence unit scanning archived competitor webpages to count occurrences of key product terms, track first-release dates, and infer promotional patterns for strategic positioning.
- SEO consultant auditing historical site snapshots to extract keyword density, publication timestamps, and backlink publisher clues from saved HTML to optimize on-page content and refresh outdated pages.
- Compliance officer reviewing stored HTML policy documents to locate regulatory terms, confirm enactment years, and identify issuing bodies for audit readiness and gap analysis.
- Genealogy researcher mining downloaded obituary and local history pages to extract names, vital dates, and relationship mentions for automated family-tree construction.

from collections import Counter

print(f'Extracted text size: {len(page_text):,} characters')

'martineau': 0,

for j, sent in enumerate(author_sentences[:2], 1):

sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text)

if '1851' in sentence and any(word in sentence for word in ['book', 'letters', 'work', 'published', 'wrote']):
if len(sentence.strip()) > 10:
year_sentences.append(sentence.strip()[:200])

if year_sentences:
patterns_found.append('1851 with book context')

for j, sent in enumerate(year_sentences[:2], 1):

# Pattern 3: Topic terms (phrenology, mesmerism, naturalism)
topic_terms = ['phrenology', 'mesmerism', 'naturalism', 'atheistic']
topic_mentions = []
for topic in topic_terms:

# Look for publisher names near 2009
publishers = [

'yale university press', 'princeton university press', 'university of chicago press',

'dover publications', 'penguin classics', 'everyman library', 'cambridge', 'oxford',
'norton', 'vintage', 'anchor books', 'university press'
]

found_publishers = []
for pub in publishers:
if pub in page_text:
# Check if publisher appears near 2009
pub_index = page_text.find(pub)
year_index = page_text.find('2009')
if pub_index != -1 and year_index != -1:
distance = abs(pub_index - year_index)
if distance < 500: # Within 500 characters
found_publishers.append((pub, distance))

if found_publishers:
# Sort by proximity to 2009
found_publishers.sort(key=lambda x: x[1])
analysis_results['publisher_clues'].extend([pub[0] for pub in found_publishers])
print('‚úì Found publishers near 2009:')
for pub, dist in found_publishers[:3]:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {pub} (distance: {dist} chars)')

# Store file analysis
file_analysis = {
'filename': filename,
'total_relevance': total_relevance,
'key_terms': {k: v for k, v in key_terms.items() if v > 0},

}

analysis_results['book_evidence'].append(file_analysis)

print(f'Patterns found: {len(patterns_found)}')
if patterns_found:
print(f' - {" | ".join(patterns_found)}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error analyzing {filename}: {str(e)}')

print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SUMMARY')
print('=' * 80)

# Summarize findings
total_author_mentions = len(analysis_results['author_mentions'])
total_year_confirmations = len(analysis_results['year_confirmations'])
total_topic_confirmations = len(analysis_results['topic_confirmations'])
total_reissue_info = len(analysis_results['reissue_information'])

print(f' ‚Ä¢ Publisher clues: {total_publisher_clues}')

# Analyze publisher frequency
if analysis_results['publisher_clues']:
publisher_counts = Counter(analysis_results['publisher_clues'])
print(f'\nüìö PUBLISHER ANALYSIS:')
print('Most frequently mentioned publishers near 2009:')
for pub, count in publisher_counts.most_common(5):
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {pub}: {count} mentions')

# Identify most likely publisher
top_publisher = publisher_counts.most_common(1)[0]

print(f' {i}. {info[:250]}...')

if total_author_mentions > 0: evidence_score += 20
if total_year_confirmations > 0: evidence_score += 20
if total_topic_confirmations > 0: evidence_score += 20
if total_reissue_info > 0: evidence_score += 25

# Final book identification
print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('FINAL BOOK IDENTIFICATION')
print('=' * 80)

print('üìñ IDENTIFIED BOOK:')
print(' Title: "Letters on the Laws of Man\'s Nature and Development"')

### Development Step 9: Identify 1851 Co-Authored Atheistic Naturalism Book on Phrenology and Mesmerism Reissued in 2009

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify a co-authored book from 1851 that advocated for atheistic naturalism, systematically explored phrenology and mesmerism, was controversial for these topics, and was reissued by a publisher in 2009. Search using keywords including '1851 book atheistic naturalism phrenology mesmerism co-authored', '1851 controversial book phrenology mesmerism reissued 2009', 'atheistic naturalism 1851 publication', and 'phrenology mesmerism 1851 authors'. Focus on identifying both the original 1851 publication details and the specific publisher who reissued it in 2009.

**Use Cases**:
- Rare book dealers verifying the provenance and reprint history of a mid-19th-century scientific treatise to accurately price and catalog high-value auction listings
- University library digitization teams automating the extraction of publication metadata and 2009 reissue details for public domain texts in their digital collections
- Academic researchers mapping the dissemination of pseudoscientific ideas (phrenology and mesmerism) in 1851 publications for a peer-reviewed history of science journal article
- Legal research departments cross-checking original publication dates and subsequent reprints to build evidence for copyright and public domain status in intellectual property cases
- Archivists in cultural heritage institutions compiling correspondence-based works and publisher reissue records to prioritize preservation efforts and secure conservation funding
- Educational publishers creating annotated critical editions of Victorian naturalism texts by programmatically validating author attributions, controversial topics, and modern reissue publishers
- Genealogical historians tracing ancestral contributions to social science debates by systematically identifying co-authored 19th-century publications and their 2009 republications

```
import os
import requests
import json
import time
from urllib.parse import quote_plus
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from collections import Counter
import re

print('=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR 1851 CO-AUTHORED ATHEISTIC NATURALISM BOOK ===')
print('Objective: Find co-authored 1851 book advocating atheistic naturalism with phrenology/mesmerism, reissued 2009\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# Based on historical knowledge and previous analysis, the target book is:
# "Letters on the Laws of Man's Nature and Development" by Harriet Martineau and Henry George Atkinson (1851)
print('TARGET BOOK CHARACTERISTICS:')
print('‚Ä¢ Published: 1851')
print('‚Ä¢ Co-authored by multiple authors')
print('‚Ä¢ Topic: Atheistic naturalism')
print('‚Ä¢ Contains: Phrenology and mesmerism content')
print('‚Ä¢ Controversial for these topics')
print('‚Ä¢ Reissued by a publisher in 2009')
print()

# Initialize comprehensive search results
search_results = {
'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'objective': 'Find 1851 co-authored book on atheistic naturalism with phrenology/mesmerism, reissued 2009',
'target_identification': {
'title': 'Letters on the Laws of Man\'s Nature and Development',
'authors': ['Harriet Martineau', 'Henry George Atkinson'],
'year': 1851,
'topics': ['atheistic naturalism', 'phrenology', 'mesmerism'],
'controversial': True
},
'search_methods': [],
'findings': [],
'publisher_analysis': {},
'final_conclusion': {}
}

# Headers for web requests
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36',
'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8',
'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9',
'Connection': 'keep-alive'
}

print('=== PHASE 1: TARGETED SEARCHES FOR BOOK IDENTIFICATION ===')
print('=' * 70)

# Comprehensive search queries targeting the specific book
targeted_queries = [
'"Letters on the Laws of Man\'s Nature and Development" Martineau Atkinson 1851',
'Harriet Martineau Henry Atkinson Letters 1851 atheistic naturalism controversial',
'"Laws of Man\'s Nature Development" phrenology mesmerism 1851 co-authored',
'Martineau Atkinson 1851 Letters atheism naturalism phrenology mesmerism',
'"Letters Laws Man Nature Development" 2009 reissue publisher edition reprint'
]

print(f'Executing {len(targeted_queries)} comprehensive searches:')
for i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1):
print(f' {i}. {query}')

# Execute searches and collect results
for i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1):
print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(targeted_queries)}: {query}')
print('-' * 60)

try:
# Google search
google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {google_url}')

response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
# Save HTML
filename = f'comprehensive_search_{i}_{query[:40].replace(" ", "_").replace("\'", "").replace('"', "")}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)

with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)

print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Parse and analyze content
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')
page_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True).lower()

# Define key terms with weights for relevance scoring
key_terms = {
'martineau': 5,
'atkinson': 5,
'1851': 6,
'letters': 4,
'nature': 2,
'development': 3,
'atheistic': 5,
'naturalism': 5,
'phrenology': 5,
'mesmerism': 5,
'controversial': 4,
'2009': 6,
'reissue': 5,
'reprint': 4,
'publisher': 4,
'edition': 3
}

# Calculate relevance and find terms
found_terms = []
relevance_score = 0
term_counts = {}

for term, weight in key_terms.items():
count = page_text.count(term)
if count > 0:
found_terms.append(f'{term}({count})')
relevance_score += weight * count
term_counts[term] = count

print(f'Relevance score: {relevance_score}')
print(f'Found terms: {" ".join(found_terms[:10])}')

# Extract meaningful text snippets
meaningful_snippets = []

# Look for sentences containing key combinations
sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text)

for sentence in sentences:
sentence = sentence.strip()
if len(sentence) > 20 and len(sentence) < 300:
# Check for author combinations
if 'martineau' in sentence and 'atkinson' in sentence:
meaningful_snippets.append(('authors', sentence))
# Check for year + book context
elif '1851' in sentence and any(word in sentence for word in ['letters', 'book', 'work', 'published']):
meaningful_snippets.append(('year_book', sentence))
# Check for topic combinations
elif any(topic in sentence for topic in ['phrenology', 'mesmerism', 'naturalism']) and any(word in sentence for word in ['controversial', 'atheistic', 'scientific']):
meaningful_snippets.append(('topics', sentence))
# Check for 2009 reissue info
elif '2009' in sentence and any(word in sentence for word in ['reissue', 'reprint', 'edition', 'publisher']):
meaningful_snippets.append(('reissue', sentence))

# Look for publisher information specifically
publishers_found = []
if '2009' in page_text:
print('‚úì Found 2009 - scanning for publishers...')

# Academic and commercial publishers
publisher_list = [
'cambridge university press', 'oxford university press', 'harvard university press',
'yale university press', 'princeton university press', 'university of chicago press',
'routledge', 'palgrave macmillan', 'sage publications', 'academic press',
'dover publications', 'penguin classics', 'everyman library', 'vintage books',
'anchor books', 'norton', 'university press', 'scholarly press',
'cambridge', 'oxford', 'harvard', 'yale', 'princeton'
]

for pub in publisher_list:
if pub in page_text:
# Check proximity to 2009
pub_positions = [m.start() for m in re.finditer(pub, page_text)]
year_positions = [m.start() for m in re.finditer('2009', page_text)]

for pub_pos in pub_positions:
for year_pos in year_positions:
distance = abs(pub_pos - year_pos)
if distance < 1000: # Within 1000 characters
publishers_found.append((pub, distance))
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {pub} (distance from 2009: {distance} chars)')
break

'query': query,
'relevance_score': relevance_score,
'term_counts': term_counts,
'found_terms': found_terms,
'meaningful_snippets': meaningful_snippets[:5], # Top 5 snippets
'publishers_near_2009': publishers_found,
'html_file': filepath,
'has_2009': '2009' in page_text,
'has_authors': 'martineau' in page_text and 'atkinson' in page_text,
'has_year': '1851' in page_text,
'has_topics': any(topic in page_text for topic in ['phrenology', 'mesmerism', 'naturalism'])
}

search_results['findings'].append(finding)
search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google search: {query} - Status {response.status_code}')

# Display key findings
if relevance_score >= 20:
print('üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE RESULT')
if meaningful_snippets:
print('Key snippets found:')
for snippet_type, snippet in meaningful_snippets[:3]:
print(f' [{snippet_type}] {snippet[:150]}...')

else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting

print('\n=== PHASE 2: FOCUSED 2009 REISSUE PUBLISHER SEARCH ===')

moderate_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if 5 <= f.get('relevance_score', 0) < 20]
reissue_focused = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('type') == 'reissue_focused']

print(f'\nüìä FINDINGS BREAKDOWN:')

print(f' ‚Ä¢ Reissue-focused results: {len(reissue_focused)}')

for finding in search_results['findings']:
if finding.get('publishers_near_2009'):
for pub, distance in finding['publishers_near_2009']:
all_publishers.append(pub)

# Analyze publisher frequency
if all_publishers:
publisher_counts = Counter(all_publishers)
search_results['publisher_analysis'] = {
'total_mentions': len(all_publishers),
'unique_publishers': len(set(all_publishers)),
'frequency_ranking': dict(publisher_counts.most_common())
}

print(f'\nüìö PUBLISHER ANALYSIS:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total publisher mentions near 2009: {len(all_publishers)}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Unique publishers found: {len(set(all_publishers))}')

if publisher_counts:
print(' ‚Ä¢ Top publishers by frequency:')
for pub, count in publisher_counts.most_common(5):
print(f' - {pub}: {count} mentions')

top_publisher = publisher_counts.most_common(1)[0]
search_results['publisher_analysis']['most_likely_2009_publisher'] = top_publisher[0]
print(f'\nüéØ MOST LIKELY 2009 PUBLISHER: {top_publisher[0]} ({top_publisher[1]} mentions)')

'book_title_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if 'letters' in str(f.get('term_counts', {})).lower()),
'authors_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_authors', False)),
'year_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_year', False)),
'topics_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_topics', False)),
'reissue_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_2009', False))
}

for evidence_type, count in evidence_summary.items():
status = '‚úÖ' if count > 0 else '‚ùå'
print(f' {status} {evidence_type.replace("_", " ").title()}: {count} findings')

search_results['final_conclusion']['evidence_summary'] = evidence_summary

# Calculate overall confidence
total_evidence = sum(evidence_summary.values())
max_possible = len(evidence_summary) * total_findings
confidence_percentage = (total_evidence / max_possible * 100) if max_possible > 0 else 0

print(f'\nüìà OVERALL CONFIDENCE: {confidence_percentage:.1f}%')
search_results['final_conclusion']['confidence_percentage'] = confidence_percentage

import os import requests import json import time from urllib.parse import quote_plus from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from collections import Counter import re print('=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR FRANTZ FUNCK-BRENTANO HISTORICAL SERIES ===') print('Objective: Find historical series by Frantz Funck-Brentano covering:') print('1. Political transition between Bourbon Restoration and July Monarchy') print('2. Gaul\'s history under Celtic, Roman, and Frankish rule') print() # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize comprehensive search results search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Frantz Funck-Brentano historical series covering Bourbon-July Monarchy transition and Gaul history', 'target_characteristics': { 'author': 'Frantz Funck-Brentano', 'format': 'Historical series', 'content_1': 'Bourbon Restoration to July Monarchy political transition', 'content_2': 'Gaul history under Celtic, Roman, and Frankish rule', 'requirement': 'At least one volume by Funck-Brentano' }, 'search_methods': [], 'findings': [], 'series_candidates': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } # Headers for web requests headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } print('TARGET SERIES CHARACTERISTICS:') print('‚Ä¢ Author: Frantz Funck-Brentano (at least one volume)') print('‚Ä¢ Format: Multi-volume historical series') print('‚Ä¢ Content Area 1: Bourbon Restoration ‚Üí July Monarchy transition') print('‚Ä¢ Content Area 2: Gaul under Celtic, Roman, and Frankish rule') print('‚Ä¢ Scope: Comprehensive French historical coverage') print() print('=== PHASE 1: AUTHOR-FOCUSED SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 50) # Execute author-focused searches for i, query in enumerate(author_queries, 1): print(f'\nAuthor Search {i}/{len(author_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Google search google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' print(f'URL: {google_url}') response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: # Parse and analyze content soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True).lower() # Define key terms with weights for relevance scoring key_terms = { 'funck-brentano': 8, 'frantz': 6, 'historical': 3, 'series': 5, 'volumes': 4, 'bourbon': 5, 'restoration': 5, 'july': 4, 'monarchy': 5, 'gaul': 6, 'celtic': 5, 'roman': 4, 'frankish': 5, 'france': 3, 'french': 3, 'history': 2, 'transition': 4, 'political': 3 } # Calculate relevance and find terms found_terms = [] relevance_score = 0 term_counts = {} for term, weight in key_terms.items(): count = page_text.count(term) if count > 0: found_terms.append(f'{term}({count})') relevance_score += weight * count term_counts[term] = count print(f'Relevance score: {relevance_score}') print(f'Found terms: {" ".join(found_terms[:12])}') # Extract meaningful text snippets meaningful_snippets = [] # Look for sentences containing key combinations sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) for sentence in sentences: sentence = sentence.strip() if len(sentence) > 25 and len(sentence) < 400: # Check for author + series context if 'funck-brentano' in sentence and any(word in sentence for word in ['series', 'volumes', 'historical', 'collection']): meaningful_snippets.append(('author_series', sentence)) # Check for Bourbon/July Monarchy context elif any(term in sentence for term in ['bourbon', 'july monarchy', 'restoration']) and any(word in sentence for word in ['transition', 'political', 'history']): meaningful_snippets.append(('bourbon_july', sentence)) # Check for Gaul history context elif 'gaul' in sentence and any(term in sentence for term in ['celtic', 'roman', 'frankish']): meaningful_snippets.append(('gaul_history', sentence)) # Check for series names elif any(phrase in sentence for phrase in ['histoire de france', 'french history', 'historical series']) and 'funck-brentano' in sentence: meaningful_snippets.append(('series_name', sentence)) # Look for potential series titles series_titles_found = [] series_patterns = [ r'histoire de france[^.]{0,50}', r'french history[^.]{0,50}', r'historical series[^.]{0,50}', r'collection[^.]{0,50}funck-brentano', r'funck-brentano[^.]{0,50}series' ] for pattern in series_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) for match in matches[:3]: # Limit to first 3 matches per pattern if len(match.strip()) > 10: series_titles_found.append(match.strip()) if series_titles_found: print('‚úì Potential series titles found:') for j, title in enumerate(series_titles_found[:3], 1): print(f' {j}. {title[:100]}...') # Store comprehensive finding finding = { 'query': query, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'term_counts': term_counts, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'meaningful_snippets': meaningful_snippets[:5], # Top 5 snippets 'series_titles_found': series_titles_found, 'html_file': filepath, 'has_author': 'funck-brentano' in page_text, 'has_series': 'series' in page_text or 'volumes' in page_text, 'has_bourbon_july': any(term in page_text for term in ['bourbon', 'july monarchy', 'restoration']), 'has_gaul': 'gaul' in page_text and any(term in page_text for term in ['celtic', 'roman', 'frankish']) } search_results['findings'].append(finding) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google author search: {query} - Status {response.status_code}') # Quick analysis for series information soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text().lower() # Look for series indicators series_indicators = ['series', 'collection', 'volumes', 'tome', 'volume'] author_indicators = ['funck-brentano', 'frantz'] has_series = any(indicator in page_text for indicator in series_indicators) has_author = any(indicator in page_text for indicator in author_indicators) if has_series and has_author: print(' ‚úì Found series + author combination') # Extract relevant sentences sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) relevant_sentences = [] for sentence in sentences: if len(sentence.strip()) > 20: if any(indicator in sentence for indicator in series_indicators) and any(indicator in sentence for indicator in author_indicators): relevant_sentences.append(sentence.strip()[:150]) if relevant_sentences: print(f' Found {len(relevant_sentences)} relevant sentences') for j, sent in enumerate(relevant_sentences[:2], 1): print(f' {j}. {sent}...') # Store topic finding search_results['findings'].append({ 'query': query, 'type': 'topic_focused', 'relevant_sentences': relevant_sentences[:5], 'html_file': filepath, 'has_series_author': True }) elif has_series: print(' ‚Ä¢ Found series indicators (no author)') elif has_author: print(' ‚Ä¢ Found author indicators (no series)') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) print('\n=== PHASE 3: ACADEMIC AND SCHOLARLY SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 55) # Academic database searches academic_sites = [ 'site:jstor.org', 'site:archive.org', 'site:hathitrust.org', 'site:gallica.bnf.fr' # French National Library ] base_query = 'Frantz Funck-Brentano historical series French history' for i, site in enumerate(academic_sites, 1): query = f'{site} {base_query}' print(f'\nAcademic Search {i}: {query}') try: # import os import requests import json import time from urllib.parse import quote_plus from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from collections import Counter import re print('=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR FRANTZ FUNCK-BRENTANO HISTORICAL SERIES ===') print('Objective: Find historical series by Frantz Funck-Brentano covering:') print('1. Political transition between Bourbon Restoration and July Monarchy') print('2. Gaul\'s history under Celtic, Roman, and Frankish rule') print() # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize comprehensive search results search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Frantz Funck-Brentano historical series covering Bourbon-July Monarchy transition and Gaul history', 'target_characteristics': { 'author': 'Frantz Funck-Brentano', 'format': 'Historical series', 'content_1': 'Bourbon Restoration to July Monarchy political transition', 'content_2': 'Gaul history under Celtic, Roman, and Frankish rule', 'requirement': 'At least one volume by Funck-Brentano' }, 'search_methods': [], 'findings': [], 'series_candidates': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } # Headers for web requests headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } print('TARGET SERIES CHARACTERISTICS:') print('‚Ä¢ Author: Frantz Funck-Brentano (at least one volume)') print('‚Ä¢ Format: Multi-volume historical series') print('‚Ä¢ Content Area 1: Bourbon Restoration ‚Üí July Monarchy transition') print('‚Ä¢ Content Area 2: Gaul under Celtic, Roman, and Frankish rule') print('‚Ä¢ Scope: Comprehensive French historical coverage') print() print('=== PHASE 1: AUTHOR-FOCUSED SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 50) # Comprehensive search queries targeting Frantz Funck-Brentano author_queries = [ 'Frantz Funck-Brentano historical series volumes French history', '"Frantz Funck-Brentano" author historical series France', 'Funck-Brentano historian French history series multi-volume', '"Frantz Funck-Brentano" Bourbon Restoration July Monarchy', 'Frantz Funck-Brentano Gaul Celtic Roman Frankish history' ] print(f'Executing {len(author_queries)} author-focused searches:') for i, query in enumerate(author_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') # Execute author-focused searches for i, query in enumerate(author_queries, 1): print(f'\nAuthor Search {i}/{len(author_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Google search google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' print(f'URL: {google_url}') response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: # Save HTML filename = f'author_search_{i}_{query[:40].replace(" ", "_").replace("\'", "").replace('"', "")}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Parse and analyze content soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True).lower() # Define key terms with weights for relevance scoring key_terms = { 'funck-brentano': 8, 'frantz': 6, 'historical': 3, 'series': 5, 'volumes': 4, 'bourbon': 5, 'restoration': 5, 'july': 4, 'monarchy': 5, 'gaul': 6, 'celtic': 5, 'roman': 4, 'frankish': 5, 'france': 3, 'french': 3, 'history': 2, 'transition': 4, 'political': 3 } # Calculate relevance and find terms found_terms = [] relevance_score = 0 term_counts = {} for term, weight in key_terms.items(): count = page_text.count(term) if count > 0: found_terms.append(f'{term}({count})') relevance_score += weight * count term_counts[term] = count print(f'Relevance score: {relevance_score}') print(f'Found terms: {" ".join(found_terms[:12])}') # Extract meaningful text snippets meaningful_snippets = [] # Look for sentences containing key combinations sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) for sentence in sentences: sentence = sentence.strip() if len(sentence) > 25 and len(sentence) < 400: # Check for author + series context if 'funck-brentano' in sentence and any(word in sentence for word in ['series', 'volumes', 'historical', 'collection']): meaningful_snippets.append(('author_series', sentence)) # Check for Bourbon/July Monarchy context elif any(term in sentence for term in ['bourbon', 'july monarchy', 'restoration']) and any(word in sentence for word in ['transition', 'political', 'history']): meaningful_snippets.append(('bourbon_july', sentence)) # Check for Gaul history context elif 'gaul' in sentence and any(term in sentence for term in ['celtic', 'roman', 'frankish']): meaningful_snippets.append(('gaul_history', sentence)) # Check for series names elif any(phrase in sentence for phrase in ['histoire de france', 'french history', 'historical series']) and 'funck-brentano' in sentence: meaningful_snippets.append(('series_name', sentence)) # Look for potential series titles series_titles_found = [] series_patterns = [ r'histoire de france[^.]{0,50}', r'french history[^.]{0,50}', r'historical series[^.]{0,50}', r'collection[^.]{0,50}funck-brentano', r'funck-brentano[^.]{0,50}series' ] for pattern in series_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) for match in matches[:3]: # Limit to first 3 matches per pattern if len(match.strip()) > 10: series_titles_found.append(match.strip()) if series_titles_found: print('‚úì Potential series titles found:') for j, title in enumerate(series_titles_found[:3], 1): print(f' {j}. {title[:100]}...') # Store comprehensive finding finding = { 'query': query, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'term_counts': term_counts, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'meaningful_snippets': meaningful_snippets[:5], # Top 5 snippets 'series_titles_found': series_titles_found, 'html_file': filepath, 'has_author': 'funck-brentano' in page_text, 'has_series': 'series' in page_text or 'volumes' in page_text, 'has_bourbon_july': any(term in page_text for term in ['bourbon', 'july monarchy', 'restoration']), 'has_gaul': 'gaul' in page_text and any(term in page_text for term in ['celtic', 'roman', 'frankish']) } search_results['findings'].append(finding) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Google author search: {query} - Status {response.status_code}') # Display key findings if relevance_score >= 25: print('üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE RESULT') if meaningful_snippets: print('Key snippets found:') for snippet_type, snippet in meaningful_snippets[:3]: print(f' [{snippet_type}] {snippet[:120]}...') else: print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting print('\n=== PHASE 2: TOPIC-SPECIFIC SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 50) # Topic-specific queries topic_queries = [ 'Bourbon Restoration July Monarchy transition historical series France', 'Gaul Celtic Roman Frankish history French historical series', '"Histoire de France" series Bourbon July Monarchy Gaul', 'French historical series political transition 19th century ancient Gaul', 'multi-volume French history Bourbon Restoration Celtic Roman Frankish' ] for i, query in enumerate(topic_queries, 1): print(f'\nTopic Search {i}: {query}') try: google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) if response.status_code == 200: filename = f'topic_search_{i}_{query[:35].replace(" ", "_").replace("\'", "").replace('"', "")}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Status: {response.status_code} | Saved: {filename}') # Quick analysis for series information soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text().lower() # Look for series indicators series_indicators = ['series', 'collection', 'volumes', 'tome', 'volume'] author_indicators = ['funck-brentano', 'frantz'] has_series = any(indicator in page_text for indicator in series_indicators) has_author = any(indicator in page_text for indicator in author_indicators) if has_series and has_author: print(' ‚úì Found series + author combination') # Extract relevant sentences sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) relevant_sentences = [] for sentence in sentences: if len(sentence.strip()) > 20: if any(indicator in sentence for indicator in series_indicators) and any(indicator in sentence for indicator in author_indicators): relevant_sentences.append(sentence.strip()[:150]) if relevant_sentences: print(f' Found {len(relevant_sentences)} relevant sentences') for j, sent in enumerate(relevant_sentences[:2], 1): print(f' {j}. {sent}...') # Store topic finding search_results['findings'].append({ 'query': query, 'type': 'topic_focused', 'relevant_sentences': relevant_sentences[:5], 'html_file': filepath, 'has_series_author': True }) elif has_series: print(' ‚Ä¢ Found series indicators (no author)') elif has_author: print(' ‚Ä¢ Found author indicators (no series)') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) print('\n=== PHASE 3: ACADEMIC AND SCHOLARLY SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 55) # Academic database searches academic_sites = [ 'site:jstor.org', 'site:archive.org', 'site:hathitrust.org', 'site:gallica.bnf.fr' # French National Library ] base_query = 'Frantz Funck-Brentano historical series French history' for i, site in enumerate(academic_sites, 1): query = f'{site} {base_query}' print(f'\nAcademic Search {i}: {query}') try: # Use Google to search specific academic sites google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}' print(f'URL: {google_url}') response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: filename = f'academic_search_{i}_{site.replace("site:", "").replace(".", "_")}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Quick analysis soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for Google result snippets snippets = soup.find_all(['span', 'div'], class_=lambda x: x and 'st' in str(x).lower()) relevant_snippets = [] for snippet in snippets: snippet_text = snippet.get_text().strip() if len(snippet_text) > 30: text_lower = snippet_text.lower() if 'funck-brentano' in text_lower and any(term in text_lower for term in ['series', 'histoire', 'history']): relevant_snippets.append(snippet_text[:200]) print(f'Found {len(relevant_snippets)} relevant academic snippets') for j, snippet in enumerate(relevant_snippets[:2], 1): print(f' {j}. {snippet}...') if relevant_snippets: search_results['findings'].append({ 'source': f'Academic - {site}', 'query': query, 'snippets': relevant_snippets, 'method': 'academic_site_search', 'html_file': filepath }) search_results['search_methods'].append(f'Academic {site}: Status {response.status_code}') else: print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(4) # Longer delay for Google print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF ALL SEARCH RESULTS') print('=' * 80) total_findings = len(search_results['findings']) print(f'Total search results collected: {total_findings}') if search_results['findings']: # Analyze by relevance high_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('relevance_score', 0) >= 25] moderate_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if 10 <= f.get('relevance_score', 0) < 25] topic_focused = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('type') == 'topic_focused'] academic_results = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if 'Academic' in f.get('source', '')] print(f'\nüìä FINDINGS BREAKDOWN:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ High relevance (25+ score): {len(high_relevance)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Moderate relevance (10-24 score): {len(moderate_relevance)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Topic-focused results: {len(topic_focused)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Academic database results: {len(academic_results)}') # Compile all series title candidates all_series_titles = [] for finding in search_results['findings']: if finding.get('series_titles_found'): all_series_titles.extend(finding['series_titles_found']) # Analyze series title frequency if all_series_titles: # Clean and normalize titles cleaned_titles = [] for title in all_series_titles: cleaned = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9\s]', ' ', title).strip().lower() if len(cleaned) > 5: cleaned_titles.append(cleaned) title_counts = Counter(cleaned_titles) search_results['series_candidates'] = dict(title_counts.most_common(10)) print(f'\nüìö SERIES TITLE ANALYSIS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total series mentions found: {len(all_series_titles)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Unique series candidates: {len(set(cleaned_titles))}') if title_counts: print(' ‚Ä¢ Top series candidates by frequency:') for title, count in title_counts.most_common(5): print(f' - "{title}": {count} mentions') # Evidence compilation evidence_summary = { 'author_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_author', False)), 'series_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_series', False)), 'bourbon_july_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_bourbon_july', False)), 'gaul_evidence': sum(1 for f in search_results['findings'] if f.get('has_gaul', False)), 'academic_evidence': len(academic_results) } print(f'\nüîç EVIDENCE SUMMARY:') for evidence_type, count in evidence_summary.items(): status = '‚úÖ' if count > 0 else '‚ùå' print(f' {status} {evidence_type.replace("_", " ").title()}: {count} findings') search_results['analysis_summary'] = evidence_summary # Calculate overall confidence total_evidence = sum(evidence_summary.values()) max_possible = len(evidence_summary) * total_findings confidence_percentage = (total_evidence / max_possible * 100) if max_possible > 0 else 0 print(f'\nüìà OVERALL CONFIDENCE: {confidence_percentage:.1f}%') search_results['analysis_summary']['confidence_percentage'] = confidence_percentage else: print('\n‚ùå No findings collected from any search method') print('This suggests the series may be:') print('1. Very specialized or not well-digitized') print('2. Known by a different name or description') print('3. Not matching our exact search terms') # Save comprehensive results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'comprehensive_funck_brentano_series_search.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Summary statistics print(f'\nüìä FINAL SEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total queries executed: {len(search_results["search_methods"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ HTML files saved: {len([f for f in search_results["findings"] if f.get("html_file")])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ High-relevance findings: {len([f for f in search_results["findings"] if f.get("relevance_score", 0) >= 25])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Series candidates identified: {len(search_results.get("series_candidates", {}))}') print('\nüéØ RECOMMENDED NEXT STEPS:') if search_results['findings']: print('1. ‚úÖ Analyze specific findings for series identification') print('2. ‚úÖ Review HTML files for additional context') print('3. ‚úÖ Cross-reference academic sources') else: print('1. üîÑ Try more specific French language searches') print('2. üîÑ Search for "Histoire de France" specifically') print('3. üîÑ Look into French academic databases') print('4. üîÑ Search for Funck-Brentano bibliography') print('5. üìã Consider library catalog searches (BnF, WorldCat)') print('6. üîç Search for French historical series from early 20th century') print('\n=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR FRANTZ FUNCK-BRENTANO SERIES COMPLETE ===')

import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re from collections import Counter print('=== ANALYZING SAVED HTML SEARCH RESULTS FOR FRANTZ FUNCK-BRENTANO SERIES ===') print('Objective: Extract information from saved HTML files to identify the historical series') print('covering Bourbon Restoration ‚Üí July Monarchy transition and Gaul history\n') # First, let's inspect what HTML files we have in the workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace' html_files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): for filename in os.listdir(workspace_dir): if filename.endswith('.html') and ('author_search_' in filename or 'funck' in filename.lower()): html_files.append(filename) print(f'Found {len(html_files)} HTML search result files:') for i, filename in enumerate(html_files, 1): filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) if os.path.exists(filepath) else 0 print(f' {i}. {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)') else: print('‚ùå Workspace directory not found') html_files = [] if not html_files: print('‚ùå No HTML search result files found to analyze') print('Need to execute searches first') else: print(f'\nüìÅ ANALYZING {len(html_files)} HTML FILES FOR SERIES INFORMATION:') print('=' * 70) # Initialize analysis results analysis_results = { 'timestamp': '2025-01-07', 'files_analyzed': len(html_files), 'series_evidence': [], 'author_mentions': [], 'bourbon_july_evidence': [], 'gaul_history_evidence': [], 'series_titles_found': [], 'volume_information': [], 'academic_references': [] } # Analyze each HTML file for i, filename in enumerate(html_files, 1): filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) print(f'\nAnalyzing File {i}: {filename}') print('-' * 50) try: with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f: html_content = f.read() # Parse HTML soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.decompose() # Extract all text content page_text = soup.get_text(separator=' ', strip=True) page_text_lower = page_text.lower() print(f'HTML file size: {len(html_content):,} characters') print(f'Extracted text size: {len(page_text):,} characters') # Look for key terms with context key_terms = { 'funck-brentano': 0, 'frantz': 0, 'historical': 0, 'series': 0, 'volumes': 0, 'bourbon': 0, 'restoration': 0, 'july': 0, 'monarchy': 0, 'gaul': 0, 'celtic': 0, 'roman': 0, 'frankish': 0, 'france': 0, 'french': 0, 'histoire': 0, 'transition': 0, 'political': 0 } # Count occurrences of each term found_terms = [] for term in key_terms.keys(): count = page_text_lower.count(term) key_terms[term] = count if count > 0: found_terms.append(f'{term}({count})') total_relevance = sum(key_terms.values()) print(f'Total term occurrences: {total_relevance}') print(f'Found terms: {" ".join(found_terms[:12])}') # Look for specific patterns and extract context patterns_found = [] # Pattern 1: Funck-Brentano with series context if 'funck-brentano' in page_text_lower: # Find sentences with author and series context sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) author_series_sentences = [] for sentence_text in sentences: # Fixed variable name sentence_lower = sentence_text.strip().lower() if 'funck-brentano' in sentence_lower: if any(word in sentence_lower for word in ['series', 'volumes', 'collection', 'histoire', 'historical']): if len(sentence_text.strip()) > 15: author_series_sentences.append(sentence_text.strip()[:300]) if author_series_sentences: patterns_found.append('Author with series context') analysis_results['author_mentions'].extend(author_series_sentences[:3]) print('‚úì Found Funck-Brentano with series context') for j, sent in enumerate(author_series_sentences[:2], 1): print(f' {j}. {sent[:150]}...') # Pattern 2: Bourbon Restoration and July Monarchy context if any(term in page_text_lower for term in ['bourbon', 'restoration', 'july monarchy']): sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) bourbon_sentences = [] for sentence_text in sentences: # Fixed variable name sentence_lower = sentence_text.strip().lower() if any(term in sentence_lower for term in ['bourbon', 'restoration', 'july']): if any(word in sentence_lower for word in ['monarchy', 'transition', 'political', 'history']): if len(sentence_text.strip()) > 20: bourbon_sentences.append(sentence_text.strip()[:300]) if bourbon_sentences: patterns_found.append('Bourbon/July Monarchy context') analysis_results['bourbon_july_evidence'].extend(bourbon_sentences[:3]) print('‚úì Found Bourbon Restoration/July Monarchy context') for j, sent in enumerate(bourbon_sentences[:2], 1): print(f' {j}. {sent[:150]}...') # Pattern 3: Gaul history context if 'gaul' in page_text_lower: sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) gaul_sentences = [] for sentence_text in sentences: # Fixed variable name sentence_lower = sentence_text.strip().lower() if 'gaul' in sentence_lower: if any(term in sentence_lower for term in ['celtic', 'roman', 'frankish', 'ancient']): if len(sentence_text.strip()) > 20: gaul_sentences.append(sentence_text.strip()[:300]) if gaul_sentences: patterns_found.append('Gaul history context') analysis_results['gaul_history_evidence'].extend(gaul_sentences[:3]) print('‚úì Found Gaul history context') for j, sent in enumerate(gaul_sentences[:2], 1): print(f' {j}. {sent[:150]}...') # Pattern 4: Look for series titles series_title_patterns = [ r'histoire de france[^.]{0,100}', r'french history[^.]{0,100}', r'historical series[^.]{0,100}', r'collection[^.]{0,100}', r'volumes?[^.]{0,50}funck-brentano', r'funck-brentano[^.]{0,50}series', r'tome[^.]{0,50}', r'volume[^.]{0,50}' ] series_titles_found = [] for pattern in series_title_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text_lower, re.IGNORECASE) for match in matches[:3]: # Limit to first 3 matches per pattern if len(match.strip()) > 10: series_titles_found.append(match.strip()) if series_titles_found: patterns_found.append(f'Series titles: {len(series_titles_found)} found') analysis_results['series_titles_found'].extend(series_titles_found) print('‚úì Found potential series titles:') for j, title in enumerate(series_titles_found[:3], 1): print(f' {j}. {title[:100]}...') # Pattern 5: Look for volume information volume_patterns = [ r'volume\s+\d+[^.]{0,100}', r'tome\s+\d+[^.]{0,100}', r'vol\.?\s+\d+[^.]{0,100}', r'\d+\s+volumes?[^.]{0,100}' ] volume_info_found = [] for pattern in volume_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text_lower, re.IGNORECASE) for match in matches[:3]: if len(match.strip()) > 5: volume_info_found.append(match.strip()) if volume_info_found: patterns_found.append(f'Volume info: {len(volume_info_found)} found') analysis_results['volume_information'].extend(volume_info_found) print('‚úì Found volume information:') for j, vol_info in enumerate(volume_info_found[:3], 1): print(f' {j}. {vol_info[:80]}...') # Store file analysis file_analysis = { 'filename': filename, 'total_relevance': total_relevance, 'key_terms': {k: v for k, v in key_terms.items() if v > 0}, 'patterns_found': patterns_found, 'has_funck_brentano': key_terms['funck-brentano'] > 0, 'has_series_context': any(key_terms[term] > 0 for term in ['series', 'volumes', 'historical']), 'has_bourbon_july': any(key_terms[term] > 0 for term in ['bourbon', 'restoration', 'july', 'monarchy']), 'has_gaul': key_terms['gaul'] > 0 } analysis_results['series_evidence'].append(file_analysis) print(f'Patterns found: {len(patterns_found)}') if patterns_found: print(f' - {" | ".join(patterns_found)}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error analyzing {filename}: {str(e)}') print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SUMMARY') print('=' * 80) # Summarize findings total_author_mentions = len(analysis_results['author_mentions']) total_bourbon_evidence = len(analysis_results['bourbon_july_evidence']) total_gaul_evidence = len(analysis_results['gaul_history_evidence']) total_series_titles = len(analysis_results['series_titles_found']) total_volume_info = len(analysis_results['volume_information']) print(f'üìä EVIDENCE SUMMARY:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Author mentions (Funck-Brentano with series): {total_author_mentions}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Bourbon/July Monarchy evidence: {total_bourbon_evidence}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Gaul history evidence: {total_gaul_evidence}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Series titles found: {total_series_titles}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Volume information: {total_volume_info}') # Analyze series title frequency if analysis_results['series_titles_found']: # Clean and normalize titles cleaned_titles = [] for title in analysis_results['series_titles_found']: cleaned = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9\s]', ' ', title).strip().lower() if len(cleaned) > 5: cleaned_titles.append(cleaned) title_counts = Counter(cleaned_titles) print(f'\nüìö SERIES TITLE ANALYSIS:') print('Most frequently mentioned series:') for title, count in title_counts.most_common(5): print(f' ‚Ä¢ "{title}": {count} mentions') # Identify most likely series if title_counts: top_series = title_counts.most_common(1)[0] print(f'\nüéØ MOST LIKELY SERIES: "{top_series[0]}" ({top_series[1]} mentions)') # Show best evidence examples if analysis_results['author_mentions']: print(f'\nüë§ BEST AUTHOR EVIDENCE:') for i, mention in enumerate(analysis_results['author_mentions'][:3], 1): print(f' {i}. {mention[:200]}...') if analysis_results['bourbon_july_evidence']: print(f'\nüëë BEST BOURBON/JULY MONARCHY EVIDENCE:') for i, evidence in enumerate(analysis_results['bourbon_july_evidence'][:2], 1): print(f' {i}. {evidence[:250]}...') if analysis_results['gaul_history_evidence']: print(f'\nüèõÔ∏è BEST GAUL HISTORY EVIDENCE:') for i, evidence in enumerate(analysis_results['gaul_history_evidence'][:2], 1): print(f' {i}. {evidence[:250]}...') # Calculate confidence score evidence_score = 0 if total_author_mentions > 0: evidence_score += 25 if total_bourbon_evidence > 0: evidence_score += 20 if total_gaul_evidence > 0: evidence_score += 20 if total_series_titles > 0: evidence_score += 20 if total_volume_info > 0: evidence_score += 15 print(f'\nüìà CONFIDENCE SCORE: {evidence_score}/100') # Final series identification print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('HISTORICAL SERIES IDENTIFICATION') print('=' * 80) print('üîç SEARCH OBJECTIVE RECAP:') print(' Find historical series that includes:') print(' 1. Analysis of Bourbon Restoration ‚Üí July Monarchy transition') print(' 2. Analysis of Gaul under Celtic, Roman, and Frankish rule') print(' 3. At least one volume authored by Frantz Funck-Brentano') # Based on historical knowledge, the most likely candidate is "Histoire de France" print('\nüìñ MOST LIKELY SERIES IDENTIFICATION:') print(' Series: "Histoire de France" (History of France)') print(' Format: Multi-volume historical series') print(' Author: Frantz Funck-Brentano (contributed volumes)') print(' Publisher: Likely Hachette or similar French publisher') print(' Period: Early 20th century') print(' Scope: Comprehensive French history from ancient times to modern era') print('\nüìö EXPECTED VOLUME COVERAGE:') print(' ‚Ä¢ Ancient Gaul: Celtic tribes, Roman conquest, Frankish kingdoms') print(' ‚Ä¢ Medieval France: Capetian dynasty, feudalism') print(' ‚Ä¢ Modern France: Revolution, Napoleon, Restoration') print(' ‚Ä¢ 19th Century: Bourbon Restoration ‚Üí July Monarchy transition') if evidence_score >= 40: print('\n‚úÖ SERIES IDENTIFICATION CONFIDENCE: HIGH') elif evidence_score >= 20: print('\n‚ö†Ô∏è SERIES IDENTIFICATION CONFIDENCE: MODERATE') else: print('\n‚ùì SERIES IDENTIFICATION CONFIDENCE: LOW - Additional research needed') # Save comprehensive analysis results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'funck_brentano_series_analysis.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Summary of files created print(f'\nüìÅ FILES IN WORKSPACE:') if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): all_files = [f for f in os.listdir(workspace_dir) if os.path.isfile(os.path.join(workspace_dir, f))] for file in sorted(all_files): file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f' ‚Ä¢ {file} ({file_size:,} bytes)') print('\n=== HTML ANALYSIS FOR FRANTZ FUNCK-BRENTANO SERIES COMPLETE ===')

import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re from collections import Counter print('=== ANALYZING SAVED HTML SEARCH RESULTS FOR FRANTZ FUNCK-BRENTANO SERIES ===') print('Objective: Extract information from saved HTML files to identify the historical series') print('covering Bourbon Restoration ‚Üí July Monarchy transition and Gaul history\n') # First, let's inspect what HTML files we have in the workspace workspace_dir = 'workspace' html_files = [] if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): for filename in os.listdir(workspace_dir): if filename.endswith('.html') and ('author_search_' in filename or 'funck' in filename.lower()): html_files.append(filename) print(f'Found {len(html_files)} HTML search result files:') for i, filename in enumerate(html_files, 1): filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) if os.path.exists(filepath) else 0 print(f' {i}. {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)') else: print('‚ùå Workspace directory not found') html_files = [] if not html_files: print('‚ùå No HTML search result files found to analyze') print('Need to execute searches first') else: print(f'\nüìÅ ANALYZING {len(html_files)} HTML FILES FOR SERIES INFORMATION:') print('=' * 70) # import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re from collections import Counter print('=== DEBUGGING AND ANALYZING SAVED HTML SEARCH RESULTS ===') print('Objective: Fix previous errors and extract information about Frantz Funck-Brentano historical series') print('covering Bourbon Restoration ‚Üí July Monarchy transition and Gaul history\n') # First, let's inspect the workspace directory structure workspace_dir = 'workspace' print(f'üìÅ WORKSPACE DIRECTORY INSPECTION:') print('=' * 50) if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): all_files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) html_files = [f for f in all_files if f.endswith('.html')] json_files = [f for f in all_files if f.endswith('.json')] print(f'Total files in workspace: {len(all_files)}') print(f'HTML files: {len(html_files)}') print(f'JSON files: {len(json_files)}') print(f'\nHTML FILES ({len(html_files)}):') for i, filename in enumerate(sorted(html_files), 1): filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f' {i}. {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)') print(f'\nJSON FILES ({len(json_files)}):') for i, filename in enumerate(sorted(json_files), 1): filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f' {i}. {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)') else: print('‚ùå Workspace directory not found') exit() # Check for Google search result structure search_results = soup.find_all('div', class_=lambda x: x and 'g' in x) print(f' Potential search results: {len(search_results)}') # Look for text in common Google result classes result_texts = [] for div in soup.find_all('div'): if div.get_text(strip=True): text = div.get_text(strip=True) if len(text) > 50 and 'funck' in text.lower(): result_texts.append(text[:200]) print(f' Divs containing "funck": {len(result_texts)}') if result_texts: print(' Sample relevant text:') for i, text in enumerate(result_texts[:2], 1): print(f' {i}. {text}...') except Exception as e: print(f'Error analyzing sample HTML: {str(e)}') # FIXED: Properly define this variable print(f'HTML file size: {len(html_content):,} characters') print(f'Extracted text size: {len(page_text):,} characters') # If we got very little text, try alternative extraction if len(page_text) < 500: print('‚ö†Ô∏è Low text extraction - trying alternative method') # Look for text in all elements all_elements = soup.find_all(text=True) all_text_pieces = [] for element in all_elements: text = element.strip() if text and len(text) > 3: all_text_pieces.append(text) page_text = ' '.join(all_text_pieces) page_text_lower = page_text.lower() print(f'Alternative extraction - Text size: {len(page_text):,} characters') # Count occurrences of each term file_term_counts = key_terms.copy() found_terms = [] for term in file_term_counts.keys(): count = page_text_lower.count(term) file_term_counts[term] = count key_terms[term] += count # Add to global count if count > 0: found_terms.append(f'{term}({count})') total_relevance = sum(file_term_counts.values()) print(f'Total term occurrences: {total_relevance}') print(f'Found terms: {" ".join(found_terms[:10])}') # Extract relevant sentences - FIXED: Proper variable handling relevant_sentences = [] if total_relevance > 0: # Split into sentences sentences = re.split(r'[.!?]', page_text) for sentence in sentences: # FIXED: Use 'sentence' consistently sentence_clean = sentence.strip() sentence_lower = sentence_clean.lower() if len(sentence_clean) > 20 and len(sentence_clean) < 500: # Check for relevant content relevance_score = 0 matched_terms = [] # Author mentions if 'funck-brentano' in sentence_lower: relevance_score += 10 matched_terms.append('funck-brentano') # Series context if any(term in sentence_lower for term in ['series', 'volumes', 'collection', 'histoire']): relevance_score += 5 matched_terms.extend([term for term in ['series', 'volumes', 'collection', 'histoire'] if term in sentence_lower]) # Historical periods if any(term in sentence_lower for term in ['bourbon', 'restoration', 'july', 'monarchy']): relevance_score += 5 matched_terms.extend([term for term in ['bourbon', 'restoration', 'july', 'monarchy'] if term in sentence_lower]) # Ancient history if 'gaul' in sentence_lower and any(term in sentence_lower for term in ['celtic', 'roman', 'frankish']): relevance_score += 5 matched_terms.extend([term for term in ['gaul', 'celtic', 'roman', 'frankish'] if term in sentence_lower]) if relevance_score >= 5: relevant_sentences.append({ 'text': sentence_clean, 'score': relevance_score, 'terms': matched_terms, 'file': filename }) print(f'Relevant sentences found: {len(relevant_sentences)}') # Show top relevant sentences if relevant_sentences: # Sort by relevance score relevant_sentences.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True) print('Top relevant sentences:') for j, sent_data in enumerate(relevant_sentences[:3], 1): print(f' {j}. Score {sent_data["score"]}: {sent_data["text"][:150]}...') print(f' Terms: {sent_data["terms"]}') # Add to global results analysis_results['all_relevant_text'].extend(relevant_sentences[:5]) # Store file analysis file_analysis = { 'filename': filename, 'total_relevance': total_relevance, 'key_terms': {k: v for k, v in file_term_counts.items() if v > 0}, 'relevant_sentences_count': len(relevant_sentences), 'text_size': len(page_text) } analysis_results['series_evidence'].append(file_analysis) analysis_results['files_analyzed'] += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'Error analyzing {filename}: {str(e)}') import traceback print(f'Traceback: {traceback.format_exc()}') print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('FINAL COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS') print('=' * 80) # Global term analysis print(f'üìä GLOBAL TERM ANALYSIS (across all {analysis_results["files_analyzed"]} files):') for term, count in sorted(key_terms.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True): if count > 0: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {term}: {count} occurrences') # Best evidence compilation if analysis_results['all_relevant_text']: # Sort all relevant text by score all_relevant_sorted = sorted(analysis_results['all_relevant_text'], key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True) print(f'\nüéØ BEST EVIDENCE FOUND (top {min(5, len(all_relevant_sorted))} sentences):') for i, sent_data in enumerate(all_relevant_sorted[:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Score {sent_data["score"]} | File: {sent_data["file"]}') print(f' Text: {sent_data["text"][:250]}...') print(f' Terms: {sent_data["terms"]}') # Categorize evidence author_evidence = [s for s in all_relevant_sorted if 'funck-brentano' in s['terms']] bourbon_evidence = [s for s in all_relevant_sorted if any(term in s['terms'] for term in ['bourbon', 'restoration', 'july', 'monarchy'])] gaul_evidence = [s for s in all_relevant_sorted if 'gaul' in s['terms']] print(f'\nüìö EVIDENCE CATEGORIZATION:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Author evidence (Funck-Brentano): {len(author_evidence)} sentences') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Bourbon/July Monarchy evidence: {len(bourbon_evidence)} sentences') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Gaul history evidence: {len(gaul_evidence)} sentences') else: print('\n‚ùå No relevant evidence found in search results') # Save comprehensive analysis results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'comprehensive_funck_brentano_analysis.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Final assessment total_evidence = len(analysis_results['all_relevant_text']) confidence_score = min(100, total_evidence * 10) # Scale evidence to confidence print(f'\nüìà ANALYSIS SUMMARY:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Files successfully analyzed: {analysis_results["files_analyzed"]}/{len(html_files)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total relevant sentences found: {total_evidence}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Confidence score: {confidence_score}/100') if confidence_score >= 30: print('\n‚úÖ SUFFICIENT EVIDENCE FOUND - Proceeding with series identification') else: print('\n‚ö†Ô∏è LIMITED EVIDENCE - May need additional searches or alternative approach') print('\n=== COMPREHENSIVE HTML ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===')
